                     <div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}'>
                      <p>
                       Are you a Muhlenberg student who likes to cook? Do you love to make sauce? Enter our SAUCE OFF!! Entrants will get to make their own sauce in the CR and students will get to vote on who wins during dinner on May 4! We are so excited for this event and cannot wait to see what fun recipes our entrants bring in! Want to enter? Email muhlenbergitalianclub&#064;gmail.com ASAP!

                     <div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}'>
                      <p>
                       TONIGHT AT 7 PM IN MILLER FORUM: Prof. Francesco Casetti, will deliver a talk entitled, &quot;The Space of Cinema,&quot; in which he will discuss the changing place of film in the global media landscape, as well as the ways in which space is portrayed in contemporary cinema.
                      </p>
                      <p>
                       Prof. Casetti is professor of film &amp; media at Yale University, and one of the foremost scholars of Italian cinema and film theory. The talk is free and open to the public. Dessert will follow the talk!
                      </p>
                      <p>
                       For more information on Casetti, check out
                       <a href="http://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Ffrancescocasetti.com%2F&amp;h=ATPKmQ4bNf0TORrj9R-WZ0UF8sZacG3bqneBnFZLlvVtTjPXRr8GGbhEbvSyqMvd66ffWYNAUAFAJBe6rf9yqk--QTsywgvS9s9mcCBLqxIfk_UAEzljI2CpODOzIaM&amp;enc=AZNBa7Hsgu13OevMEmWipMAQRKPkKY__qguaUczkmGzNgqLGMOnxIKVML7rkHeRZPTCVhZ9qu4VwrH3xtu036LLM32PUPEL2kI9YtALdcSHkYvHq9Ttg920fNCwd0KB2N4oA7VDRLuA7iTo5cLM10AckvAPBE8D-SeLfFYQW8tr7Jrzwqq4uU6nJJTVqbKJbCJUvlr24k8CPI3SMtXHn2uIB&amp;s=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" onmouseover='LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, "http:\/\/francescocasetti.com\/");' onclick='LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, "http:\/\/l.facebook.com\/l.php?u=http\u00253A\u00252F\u00252Ffrancescocasetti.com\u00252F&amp;h=ATPKmQ4bNf0TORrj9R-WZ0UF8sZacG3bqneBnFZLlvVtTjPXRr8GGbhEbvSyqMvd66ffWYNAUAFAJBe6rf9yqk--QTsywgvS9s9mcCBLqxIfk_UAEzljI2CpODOzIaM&amp;enc=AZNBa7Hsgu13OevMEmWipMAQRKPkKY__qguaUczkmGzNgqLGMOnxIKVML7rkHeRZPTCVhZ9qu4VwrH3xtu036LLM32PUPEL2kI9YtALdcSHkYvHq9Ttg920fNCwd0KB2N4oA7VDRLuA7iTo5cLM10AckvAPBE8D-SeLfFYQW8tr7Jrzwqq4uU6nJJTVqbKJbCJUvlr24k8CPI3SMtXHn2uIB&amp;s=1");'>
